<Z>Thursday 28th June <C> Apologies to postal players if these results are late, see below for the details.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Postal Strike <C> As I'm sure most of you have seen, the Communications Workers Union have called a National Postal Strike for<L.31.1>
Friday 29th June, with the likelihood of more to come.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
Assuming that these strikes are a series of one-day strikes, it is my intention to continue running games as normal. With the<L.31.1>
majority of players now playing via the Internet anyway they won't be affected, and I don't think it would do anyone any good if<L.31.1>
we started skipping deadlines - you want games run, and my business needs to keep running.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
I appreciate that this will cause disruption for "postal players". If at all possible, I would suggest now is the time to try and<L.31.1>
get some sort of Internet access (whether a library, mate's computer, Internet Cafe, etc). You can submit orders via<L.31.1>
www.softsim.co.uk once you've got a username (just email and ask) and results can all be sent as PDF files which can be read on<L.31.1>
pretty much any machine. If you do want to try a sample report to get it all working, just drop me an email and ask.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
For those who really are dependent on the post, then all I can do is recommend you show some patience, and foresight. If results<L.31.1>
being sent to you are delayed by a 24-hour strike, then don't assume they'll just show up the next day. I'd guess that the strike<L.31.1>
next Friday (29th June) which will affect results run the day before will mean a backlog of post they'll spend the next 3-4 days<L.31.1>
clearing, so don't be surprised if results from games run on Thursday 28th June take some time to reach you.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
As far as sending in orders, please send them in as early as possible. The overall speed of the post will be reduced with strikes<L.31.1>
about, so my recommendation that you allow at least three days for first class mail becomes more pertinent than ever. If you have<L.31.1>
to do it last minute, use the Internet or fax on 020 8249 1819.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Email Results <C> If you think results are late, please make sure you wait until the following morning before chasing up<L.31.1>
results. First step is to check out the Latest News at www.pbmsports.com - if I am running late I'll post a notice there. Please<L.31.1>
don't chase me up because you know your mate got his half an hour ago, because whilst most emails are "instant", often they do get<L.31.1>
delayed for a few hours and it does take a while to send them all out. Equally, if I am running late I don't want to be scrabbling<L.31.1>
around answering emails saying I'm running late, when I'd rather be actually getting the turns run so you don't need to chase me.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
Equally however, if it's the next morning and you've not had results, and there's nothing on www.pbmsports.com saying I've had a<L.31.1>
problem, then please chase me up. If it hasn't shown 12 hours later, odds are it won't, and probably some firewall or spam filter<L.31.1>
somewhere has gobbled it (and they do appear to do so without pattern). I'd rather you ended up with two copies than none.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>PDF Reports <C> Emailed game reports are now available for all games here. You should find PDF reports rather easier to cope<L.31.1>
with - Adobe Reader is free to download (see www.pbmsports.com for a link) and you can open your reports with one click of the<L.31.1>
mouse (indeed, you don't need a printer, though most of you will then print from it) and you don't need to worry about dodgy email<L.31.1>
clients (Hotmail and AOL are particularly common culprits) messing up the formatting, or printer drivers. The text format for<L.1.1>
<P>
<L>
<L.1.1>
emailed reports is still available but I only expect people will want to do so if they use the text file for other purposes (such<L.31.1>
as exporting the listings into some software you've produced yourself).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
If you've not tried email reports before, or you've had problems, try out the PDF. It really is very straightforward.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Credit Card Payments <C> If you want to pay by credit card over the Internet you now have the option of paying in Sterling, US<L.31.1>
Dollars or Aussie Dollars, whichever you prefer. Cheques are still fine as well, and actually mean slightly lower charges for us!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Websites <C> The website for submitting orders is at www.softsim.co.uk. www.pbmsports.com is our main "static" information<L.31.1>
website, as well as news of what's going on here. For news of what is happening with Pete in Yeovil see www.sidetracks.co.uk. For<L.31.1>
information on baseball and how it works, see www.howbaseballworks.com - a site also designed for recruiting new punters! <L.31.1>
